I came to the front desk to report the situation and requested to turn on the cooling function of the air conditioner. At this time, I happened to encounter other guests who were also negotiating with the front desk staff because of the air conditioner problem. The front desk staff told us that they will decide whether to turn on the air conditioning after consultation! Fortunately, the air conditioner in the room was able to cool down later.
When I returned to the room after breakfast the next morning, the air conditioner failed to cool again. After reporting the situation, I was told that the air conditioner was unavailable and would not be turned on until November 15th! Only one electric fan is provided! After returning to the room at night, the room temperature was always 27 degrees throughout the night. I was woken up by the heat at 4:10 in the morning and was sweating all over. I didn't fall asleep until I got up at dawn.
After staying for two nights, I was shocked and had no choice but to check out and return with a sense of failure, ending the trip early.
